partyculer werke answere fyrstely fyrst whiche suche credo deu petre omnipotente creatore celi caplm vij et terre saye byleue godres nolunt male disponi ideo vn princeps ari xii nietha fader omnypotent creatour heuen erth also noted nother thynge doctours byleue god byleue god byleue god mysbyleuers pay nems byleue god euyll crysten mencredere deu e credere ipm ee credere deo est credere byleued god parfectly byleued hym souerayne goodnes infynyte moche euery creaturesi diligit sermone meu seruabit io xu desyred appetyted loued good thynge behoued creature resonable loue god hym appetyte soueraynly hym bonte infynytediliges dnm deu tuu ex toto corde tuo et ex tota aia tua ex totis viribus tuis ex omni mete tua luce x qui ex vobis patre petit pane nu qid lapides dabit illi aut pisce nunqid pisce serpente dabit illi aut si petierit ouu nuqid porriget ei scorpione si ergo vos cu scitis mali nosc bona dare filiis ri quam magi pater vester celestis de celo dabit spiritu bonu petenti bus se luce xi yf shall kepe aboue thynges comaudementes whiche may good good syns procede bonte infynyte doth contrary kepeth comaundementes lyued good merytoriously god hym hath comaunded sayenge thou sholdest loue god thyn herte thy thought thy myght wherof sayth doctour named prosper loued god often thynkynge hy desyrynge come vnto blessyd vysyon hauynge synne hate anoyauce charge honour pleasurs worlde rychesses disprayse comparyson loue god creatour goodes whiche without ende cause loue god aboue thynge bonte infynyte moche fader omnypotent wherfore loued v childer loue loue infynyte moche almyghty behoued make gyue goodes vnto childern loue whiche loued ben goodes glory herte may thynke ne tonge declare whiche vnto v may gyue souerayne myght whiche hath created made heuen erthe well make grete wysedome wyll bonte pyteous buxomnes whiche euery man ought enforce hym byleue haue hope ende come vnto augmentacyon charyte holy merytoryous werkes saynt gregory sayth moche fayth greueth hope augmented moche man hath dyspayre man wanteth charyte good holy operacyons soo thre thynges ben alwaye egall vnto proporcion euery vertues ought haue therfore grete lytell man may truely vnderstande knowe fayth charyte hope persone none wyse therfore sayth lorde jhesu cryste gospell man knowith tree fruyte bereth good euyll fruyte procedeth tree menynge bo de floure leef entended werkes whiche proceden herte wyll eyther fayth fruyte tree lyke wyse thanfides fine ib inortua est ia ii ben twelue artycles dystyncted behoueth also twelue fruytes twelue werkes mery oryous euery answere vnto artycle werke present artycle mortalyte childely fere amerous fere whiche thynge vnto v shewed gyuen knowe vnderstande thatsi ego du ssi vbi timor si pa vbi honor malachie per timore din declinat ois homo malo item qui timet deu faciet bona eccliastici xv sayd deum patrem omnipotentem fere due vnto god whiche juste infynyte loue vnto fader almyghty fader mercy bonte infynyte euer shall haue fayth artycle herte werke sayd shall habounde good werkes withoutforth shall shewe euyll synne lyke wyse sayth holy scrypture man ought byleue fayth artycle deed bereth fruyte werke p foloweth ij artycle suche iesum cristum filium eius vnicum minum nostrum saye byleue jhesu cryst souerayne lorde sone god fader man ought vnderstande semblable egall vnto fader thynges whiche appertaynen vnto deite one self essence dyuynyte well fader sone also holy goost one god blessyd infynyte incomprehensyble dyuynyte one thre personesfaciam holem ad ymagine similitudine nostra genesis notwithstandynge made vnto ymage blessyd trynyte pryncypally vnto soule whiche mynde vnderstandynge wyll ye whiche thre myght whiche one always one essence one ymage trynyte whiche v may somwhat knowe serche thynge whiche represented blessyd trynyte howno plus sapere quam sed sae ad sobrietat vnicui que sicut deus dimisit mensura fidei ad romanos xi fides e substatia rerum speranda rum augmentu apparentiu ad heb ought byleue symply without moche curyous inquyrynge ony may ryght greuously synne offende yf fayth aboue entendement man may well vnderstande comprehende hym mysterye blessyd trynyte sholde haue neyther fayth meryte consequence myght neuer come vnto saluacyon fayth whiche none thynge god hath shewed may ought vnderstande naturally begynnynge groude saluacyon er e de certitudine adhesionis speculationis non e volutate humana allata est aliqu phetia sed spu sancto inspirati locuti sut sancti de hoy li pet wherfore behoueth vnto moost grete clerkes euer sharpe theyr naturall entendement thynges touche vnto ye hyghnes holy fayth vnto v ought suffyse knowe may may vnderstande see euery lytell creature herbe tree thynge ther neuer grete clerke phylosopher myght knowe parfectly propretecs vertues nature lytell herbe whiche foloweth greter reason may naturally knowe creature fayth whiche certayne knowlege naturall entendement god whiche may lye vnto v hath shewed holy wrytynges whiche ben owne wordes whiche hath put herte mouth holy prophetes apostle also holy martyr confessours whiche haue holden kepte trought holy fayth catholyke shedde theyr blood receyued deth joyously god hath done theyr lyf theyr deth myracles grete euydent approue trought fayth crysten man sayd myracles theyr predycacyons made solemply trought holy fayth catholyke ne ought ony thynge doubte otherwyse synned ryght greuously neythervobiscu su v que ad sumatione seculi math vltimo propietates viroru dno rum sapientia pieta vel mia potetia et nobilitas iusticia may sayd byleued stedfastly jhesu cryst sone god fader doubted fayth jhesu cryste whiche trought infynyte hath promysed shalbe wt chirche hym gyue vnto ye holy goost tyll vnto ende worlde wordes artycles vnto v ben shewed iiij pretees ye true seygnourye yt knowe wysdome swetnes mercy myght noble fourth justyce whiche sholde haue hym auowe souerayne lorde fyrst reason wysdome infynyte whiche vnto v gyuen yelde vnto body soule lyf whan one hath lost seruyce except jhesu cryst lorde lordes kynge kynges werke present artycle ye moralyte obedyence kepynge comaudement jhesu cryst intencyon ye trouth hath declared gospell entent lyterall carnall scrybes pharysees thynge without cause called hym lorde whome wyll comaudementes also hym humble loue holy pouerte euer byleued jhesu cryst god full wysedom infynyte b leued humanyte present lyf v hath gyuen example perfeccyon chosynge lyf estate whiche moost worth taketh humanyte obedyence penauce humiliauit se et ipm fact obedies v que ad mortem morte aute cruci philip ii pouerte shewynge v folowe hym whiche good crysten man catholyke hym ought meke auaryce vsury rauayne symonye forsake propre sensualyte restrayne repreue elles fayth artycle deed whiche werke bereth phere foloweth iij artycle suche qvi concept est de spiritu sancto natus exmaria virgine moche saye byleue virgyn marie conceyued sone god fader vertue holy goost bare childe virgynyte abydynge alwayes sauequi propter no hoy p nra salute descedit de celis carnatus est de sp exmaria gi e ho factus est ec symbolo hole entyere artycle declared openly credo whiche man syngeth whan sayth masse sayth loue saluacyon humayne nature ye sone god fader descended heuens toke humanyte blessyd gloryous sacred virgyn marie vertue ye blessyd holy goost makynge hym man comen downe crystenego dico tibi tu e petrus su hac petra edificabo ecclesiam mea mathei xv men whiche saynt peter confessed auowed whan sayd tu e xpristus filij dei viui thou art cryste sone lyuende god confessyd cryste knoweth hym man called hym sone god wytnesseth verely god therfore lorde hym answereth auowe trought knoweth knowe humayne nature dyuyne one persone shall founde sette trought holy fayth catholyke werke artycle moralyte conceyue sone god spyrytually vertue holy goost holy fayth catholyke interiori ho e habitare xpm de cordibus vestris ad ephe iii quicun que fecerit volutate pris mei celis e e frat soror mater est math xii meane whiche fayth jhesu cryst enhabyted within conscyences true catholykes excellently hymself wytnesseth gospell conscyence receyued true fayth ought sayd moder certayne noble dygne holy thynge conceyue hym spyrytally sholde conceyue hy corporally suche noble infelici cepit maria deu mente fide quam carnis as ptione hec aug li de gi one crysten man knowe yt conscyence yee moder god tonge may suffycyently speke vnderstandynge byleue comprehende duely adueruayll depnes deuoute comtemplatyf spyrytes erthely ought prosterne ryght humbly holy goost example fayth artycle deed fruyte honour bereth vnto fader moder phere foloweth iiij artycle suche passus sub poncio pylato crucifixus mortu et sepultus saye byleue jhesu cryst suffred deth passyon vnder ye bysshop pylate hath ben sayd true crysten man ought enforce hym thynke ye lyght holy fayth whiche one sayth thynges dyuyned thyng past beynge come suffred thynge suffred endured wherfore hy ben contrarye whiche haue done ylle synne wherof bereth payne whiche myght better whiche may hym worthely gyue thankes seluen whiche hath agayne bought whiche ryally seruytours deuyll synne true mia copiosa apd eu redeptio p c xxix soule jhesu cryst vnyed dyuynyte hath clere knowlege thynges past present com whiche behoueth confesse seeth synnes mortall euer shall done vnto ye ende worlde moche pleasure wyll blessyd trynyte yt passyon world ryght habundautly agayne bought eternall dampnacyon jhesu cryst suffred endured partyculer payne euery mortall synne euer shall done ayenst wyll dyuyne hym shall fynally sa hym shall dampned moche grete payne due vnto euery mortal synne whiche thynge surmouteth vndersta dynge create ye lyght fayth knowe suffred god whiche reasonably consente yf shedde sorowe anguysshe one oonly droppe blood yf soueraynly suffyseth redeme thousande worldes oonly hadde gyuen one droppe blood space two thyrty yeres thre monethes hath suffred endured well wombe virgyn marie also syns yt borne worlde labour paynes trauayles fastynge prayenge temptacyons contradiccyons fynally deth moost greuous pyteous dolorous yt herte may thynke naturall foly herte hondred tymes infynyte yf possyble speke ymagen ant est offensa quam tus e lle offen ethico rum parte hath ben sayd euery mortall synne euer shall done hath borne payne suffycyent repayre iniurye done vnto maieste dyuyne whiche iniurye euery synne infynyte ransome hym whiche hath offended reason nature agree moche man offendeth moost grete offence iniurye done ayenst hym moost grete ynough knowen god maieste infynyte whiche foloweth offence done ayenst hym ought infynyte consequens payne due answere vnto suche offence elles god sholde true juge dapne eternally one oonly mortall synne hym whiche defaute shall ayen bought blessyd passyon answere vnto yt folysshe ymagynacyon whiche alwayes graute lyght holy fayth yt whiche suffred god yt suffred moche god also confesse fyrst artycle demaunde estate persone yf knowe knowe yf estate maryage estate chirche reguler seculer clerke laye noble noble prelate subiecte vocacyons may forme interrogacyons synnes whiche moost comenly abounden suche people vnto people chirch symony irregularyte sacrylege euyll dyspendynge patrymonye jhesu cryste ben goodes chirche also noble peple offycers rauayn vnto people marchau de offrandes lyenges synne synner ought tell confesse yf vnto hym possyble nere vnto hym may semblable thynges dyscrecyon medyfycacyon sayd whiche appereth confessour ought haue thre thynges scyence cautelle dyscrecyon scyence dyscerne dyuersytees maner synnes cautelle enquyre axe questyons dyscrecyon gyue enioyne penaunce ellys hym dysposeth vnto grete peryl well saluacyon confesseth also ought warne hy confesseth name acuse another persone thanne hymself yf synne suche condycyon otherwyse may sayd declared ought dyscende moche partyculer cyrcumstaunces synnes specyally synne lechery may come lettyge conscyence cometh vnto ende confessyon synner hath parfytly tolde declared synnes interrogacyons wyse confessour oughte hym shewe errour greuousnesse synnes also grace god vnto hym hath done hath abyden hym penaunce hym loue fynally good purpose yf vnto hym possyble good hope mercy god case ceason may hym assoyle case excomyny ge wyll pardonne seche pardonne make restytucyon case hym ought counseyll forme manere fynde remedy hym recomaunde vnto sacred vyrgyn mary foutayne pyte mercy doynge ony good dedys soo doynge god hym shall soner helpe fynde remedyes also yf confessour knoweth ony sygnes lokynges coniectures waye synner sayeth suffysauntly synnes hym ought warne alonely one tyme many yf leue ony thynge vnto wyttynge confessyon confessyon synneth greuously hym ought warne go another confessour retorne hym another tyme may haue dyspocysyon also confessour wyse dyscrete enioyne penaunce vnto synner wyll receyue wylfully whiche semblable shal accomplysshe shewynge hym yf forgytful nesse otherwyse wyll accomplysshe excepteth may wel synneth greuously bounden suche case confesse hym also neuer synne secrete ought gyue open penaunce whiche ben confessed ought kepe well mockery malyce cursyd cause thenne shewe secrete confessyon soo doynge synne greuously yf ony persone hy fele strongly roted ony synne may bounde good dyscrecyon vnto soules payne temporall case retorne vnto synne swere without cause lechery synne fordfie pauci saluantur pe dixit ad illos contedite intrare per angusta port dico vobis quam multi queret itrare et non potuerut luce xiii somtyme many kepe theym well retorne vnto synne fere losse x shelynges ye peny halfe peny whiche kepeth loue god thynge pleasaunt vnto god whan persone secheth wayes maners correcte hym punysshe synnes please god creatour many ben blyndyd knowlege loue god greuousnesse synne peryll euyll custome payn hell glory paradyseitem gre justu est vt voluit penitere cum potu cu voluerit r sit whiche shall dylygent hym make hole ache tothe remedy thynge whiche hangeth theyr dampnacyon whiche happeneth oftymes suche fynde remedy whan desyre wolde whan may well fynde wyll thynges sayd appereth clerely arte scyence well justly examyne theyr conscyence vnto saluacyon well confessour hym whiche confessed hygh subtylyte strayt byleue scyence humayne alonely study clergy man may well iustley acquyte without synguler ayde blessed holy goost whiche aydeth techeth whiche ordynauce holy chirche ben fere humylyte charyte poore soules receyuen offyce confessour ye contrary whiche presumpcyon couetyse ther causesi cecus ceco ducatuprestat ambo foueam cadunt math iugen vnto suche offyce fallen conuenyent whiche sayth lorde yf one blynde man ledeth tweyne fallen dyche phere foloweth scyence necessary vnto confessour caplm vii foloweth c specyall scyencecu ante sit ar ar tiu regime aiarum vt extra de eta et qua ordinadorum ignominiosum fore alde couicitur clericos ad hoc regime motos ca ipsius reg mi p n tus ignorare na vilis im co putadus est nisi p c dat scia scitate alii prestacior e honore q vilismus scia quide sacerdotib ad mod est necessaria iuxta ii ld malachie ii labium sacerdotu custodiut scia lege ex rut scil ud diti ex ore vt extra cu ex ucta xi q sacerdo tibus xliii di sed ctor cyrcumspeccyon ought haue whiche excercyseth offyce confessoure ye confessour iuge co scyence ye synner may gyue good sentence behoueth haue knowlege dyscrecyon aduysynge yf synne mortall venyall therfore vnderstonde dyfference synne well noted holy chirche hath two maner comaundementes fyrst maner vnto v ordeyned duely well ageyne god agayne neyghbour ben named x commaundementes lawe whiche hath ben treatyd whiche knowe euery persone hath wytte age dyscressyon delyberacyon fully consentynge equyualent trespasseth ony x commaundementes synneth mortally breketh charyte whiche lyfe spyrytuall soule meane loue god oure neyghbour may excused ygnoraunce yf doute ony case partyculer touchynge commaundementes god ought enformed whiche haue fere god knowlege lawe put hym ye peryll transgressyon synne mortally wyse sayen doctours holy scrypture suche persone dyspyseth god saluacyon whiche thynge may creature resonable without gylt dedely synne seconde maner commaundementes ben ordynaunces statute humayne prelate holy chirche lordes whiche may haue auctoryte make lawes ordynaunces yt subiectes ought kepe accomplysshe ye true intencyon theyr souerayns transgressyon suche ordynauces shall alwayes dedely synne yf dyspysynge whiche haue made sayd ordynaunces commaundement moche grete notable exces thynge whiche hymself venyall synne yf sayd exces contenement therfore ryght syngulerly noted neuer man ne ought juge ony synne mortall yf comyttyd delyberacyon full consent sayth equyualent say equyualent moche many synnen habytacyon custome contempte whiche ben blyndyd maner semeth vnto dyspose gyue theyr consent many thynges whiche ben vnprouffytable whiche alwayes doctours ben synes dedely ye custome swere thyng without cause resonable vndyscretly agayne comaundementes souerayns rule generall well thynges sayd folowen also confessour ought dyscerne aduyse yf synner fallen sentence excome ged interdyted may ryne well clerkes laye people yf suspended irreguler whiche alonely vnto clerkes yf hediscretus quere dus e sacerdos sciens soluere ligare de pe quem penitet vi qui vult et c placuit e de pe oes c vlt de symoni ex diligenti et secudu aug caue sput iuder vt si cut non misit crime ne e ita non careat muere scie oportet ei vt sciat discernere id e qd det iudicare qr iudiciaria potestas hoc expostulat vt qd debet iudicare discernat de pe vi c viciu enim magnu e ab aliis querere seu discere q ipsos iudica eloqui decet vt ant coll vi de iudi vbi illi q vii excomenged confessour may hym assoyle sacramentally tyll vnto losed assoyled sayd sentence therfore confessour ought take hede yf haue auctoryte yf absolucyon appertayn vnto pope vnto bysshop vnto nother juge ecclesy astycall entent counseyll synner ought fynde remedy also ought dyscerne bytwene dyuers espyces maners synne mortall suffyseth hym confesse generall hym behoueth tell cyrcustau ce whiche may gretely greue chau ge synne dyuers espyces therfore sayeth well mayster wyllyam durande yf confessour soo lytell knowynge fuffyseth dyscerne synnes cyrcumstauces theym sayd synner ought confesse hym another yf suche wyse lettred meane soo dyscrete may supply suffysauce confessour also ouer sayd confessour ought conne dyscerne knowe yf bataylles prynces ben juste vniuste also tax imposycyons subsydes exaccyons yf rauen couenientibus cec aut si cec ducatu psterabo fouea cadut math xv c xxx vii di c vlti xxxviii q ipis ignora tia etei est oim errorum xxxviii di ca vn sedm augu danabilis fecto est ignora cia sacerdotu vbi hnt quo valeant eru diri xxxvii di st n ca vlt also sellynges byenges contractes yf ben vniuste otherwyse may justely enioy ne restytucyon whiche necessyte true absolucyon also ought haue knowlege wo e testametes case symony vseryes dyffycultes whyche oftymes come dede confessyon suffycyent know dyscerne juge thynges sayd enforme replenysshe synner vnto knowynge shewe hys remedyes ellys vnto ye grete peryll dapnacyon well hymself co fesseth also whiche hym gaue fyce whiche may sholde proue yf excercyse confessyons therfore sayth holy euangelyst yf one blynde man lede another two fallen dyche vnderstonde yt consecracyon presthode euery preste receyueth keyes jurysdyccyon puyssauce assoyle may excercyse yf haue mater subgecte people holy chirche therfore behoueth haue auctoryte comen ryght holy fader ye pope bysshoppes diocesains curate theyr parysshynges hath sayd auctoryte preuylege lycence one thre sayd sy ner hath lycence preuylege confessour wyse dyscrete elles yf absolucyon made without iurysdyccyon sholde true absolucyon synnen mortally well prest whiche confessed whan holely also good noted yt doctour named austen anchone ra ihabytacion presumpcyon wyll hym vnto whiche aperteyneth gyue jurysdyccyon confesse hath power place suche case sholde folowe absolucyon synnes sholde dyspence thynge whiche may whiche certaynte may true absolucyon lyke wyse appereth reason ye sayd doctour put noted wytnes layd boke p folowen case whiche absolucyon caplm viii aug de anchona de ptate pape dicit quam rati habicio h lo u absolucoe sacramentali ad que requirut tria mo p ex pi ordis susceptione sedo ordis executo ex superioris iurisdiccoe tercio sacramenti admistraco exipsius verbi cum elemeto aplicatoe qr applicat verbum adelemetu sit sacrametu sedm augu si ergo aliquis sacerdos aliquem absoluit tu e rite absolut qr talus absolucione deficit ex te sacerdotis orbis execucio et si post mod ex tesuioris su ueniat rati habicio defici sacramenti applicacio talis rati habicio valet qui si papa exsola rati habicoe ab sacrameti applicato ne po alique absoluete po effectu sacrameti ab que sacto conferre qd xpus nulli puto homini cocessit ec augustinus p fatu reserued vnto pope whiche ought knowe note whiche heren confessyons resolucyon doctours euery persone whiche stryketh malycyously ony clerke relygyous man relegyous woman suche maner stroke betynge ryght may sayd cruell wrongfull excomunycate sentence papall also breneth ony holy place relegyon falleth renneth sentence papall bysshoppe dyocesayn hym denouceth excomunycate sayd denoucyacyon bysshop hym may assoyle soo brenneth place house prophanes excomunycate tyll vnto tyme bysshop hym maketh denouced suche cause afterwarde may assoyled auctoryte pope also yf falsefye letter pope theym puttynge takynge one letter one poynt one mynyme vse suche letter malycyously excomunycate sentence papall also whiche ben parteners vnto cryme ony persone hath ronne sentence papall geuynge ayde coforte fauour vnto sayd cryme renne semblable sentence also ben receyuen wyttyngly vnto sacramentes chirche vnto sepulture ecclesyastycall also whiche otherwyse letteth procede god good conscyence agayne ony heretyke whiche putteth cursydly cryme heresy vnto ony man ellys euer letteth malycyously offyce sayd inquysycyon ben excomunycate case pope sacramentes holy chirche rennen semblable sentence also euer hym maketh assoyled artycle deth ony sentence cursynge payne canonycall pope bysshop juge ecclesyastycall escapeth sayd peryll artycle boun de hym represent vnto hym whiche hym may assoyle sayd artycle peryll shall haue oportunyte vnto dothe case sayd sentence jugement dyscrecyon absoluant wyse agayne falleth maner sentence wherof hath ben assoyled sayd artycle deth another thynge sholde absolucyon sacramentall synnes whiche hath ben assoyled sayd artycle shall bounde necessyte hym reconfesse notwithstandynge absolutyon apparteyne vnto pope vnto bysshop also herytykes whiche vnto gyuen ayde socours comfort ben acursyd case pope also preestes ben regulers seculers whiche warnen ony persone swere vowe promes good fayth otherwyse case reseruyd vnto bysshop case reserued vnto bysshop well ryght aucyent custome ben ix knowe foure ryght v auncyent custome fyrst synne ony derke sholde irryguler whiche may come four maners fyrst statute ordynaunces prouyncyalles synne defended vpon payne cursynge freers sayd may assoyle absolucyon cursynge apperteyneth ryght vnto bysshoppes excepte whiche ben reserued vnto holy fader also well noted preste whiche receyueth wyttyngly persone acursed grete cursynge offyce ye chirche ony sacramentes sepulture ecclesyastycall synne mortally suspended admynystracyon ecclesyastycall et fil et spiritus santi amen reason holde forme moche whiche ben sentence parteners sacramentes holy chirche whome sacrament enhybyt tyl vnto ben loused sayd sentence lyke wyse appereth ryght also noted yt may well assoyled paynes canonycalles ben excomunye suspencyon interdyte irrygularyte without assoyled sacramentally synnes one sayd paynes abydynge boude yf bounde many absolucyon sacramentall whiche behoueth assoyled synnes one cause reason wherfore man may comen ben acursyd without ennynge ye sentence conteyned vers vtile lex humile re ignorata necesse hec anathema quidem fa defended vpon payne synne ne sentence phere foloweth dystyncyon thre manere penaunce thre maner penauce ben well ryght caplm x custome vnderstonde ope penaunce solempne penauce penauce secrete holy concylle sayth mayster wyllyam durande scot moche suche penauce may sooner come sclander prouffyte edyfycacyon soules therfore man shold punysshe whiche begge trewande go thorowe worlde naked betynge hym self people affermynge yt vnto hath ben enioyned penauce whiche lyen falsely cursydly penauce solepne yt man begyneth assewenesdaye grete mystery ought gyuen grete synnes open wrongfull apperteyneth alonely vnto bysshop gyue vnto hym whiche hym representeth forme maner enioyne di si depost remissione ff enul aliqua vno e co gr que also te pore necessa also suche penaunce wryten ryght pope curate whiche may assoyle parysshynges case whiche reserued ryght custome vnto pope vnto bysshop vnto preestes reguler seculer whiche comyssyon generall specyally auctoryte lycence one thre sayd also cyrcumstaunces whiche may chaunge synne dyuers maners synne thefte man ought take hede yf culpable vseryes symonyes fals weyghtes mesures rauens sacryleges whiche wyttyngly malyce alonely accuse alonely thefte haue comytted sacrylege extorcyon vsery well confessed synne mortally lyke wyse synne lechery hym accuseth fornycacyon hath comytted auoutry incest defloracyon sacrylege espyces confessed synnen mortally therfore persone whiche confessed ought tell clerely case yf syple confessour hy ought declare greef hardnes hys case p folowen x poyntes one whiche many confessyon may thynge also instruccyon examen well hym whiche sacrament maryage thynges sayd persone wyll make good confessyon vnto helth souleought well take hede vnto x poyntes folowen one many cofessyon may thynge fyrst yt ye sentence cursyng yf holy chirche hath power hym assoyle ony mortall synne tyll vnto loused otherwyse partener sacramentes holy chirche seconde poynt yt synner ought take hede make conscyence ought made make ought made defaute poyntes confessyon may nothynge oft tymes happeneth vnto many make conscyence case vseryes symonyes gyftes whiche make otherwyse lyberall loue also cursyd wylles dysposed synne mortall whan haue put effect haue lefte loue fere god alonely fere worldely fere tobe dampned elles haue place tyme oportunyte also haue coplysshed werkes mercy place tyme man boude comaundement god vpon payne dedely synne ye whiche thynge harde vnto symple people vnderstonde dyscrecyon good aduysement cofessours doctryne treatyse precedent werkes mercy also hath taught corrected man bounde correcte place tyme also whan man oweth lawfully ony thynge man hath well power pay vnto whome man oweth willeth requyreth payed dettour hath justyce excusacyon sholde may paye suche redeuable contynually estate dedely synne may assoyled yf haue wyll acquyte hym sone may appereth culpe many symple ygnoraunt confessours whiche case semblables make conscyence vnto assoylen many ofte tymes owen poore people whiche defaute theyr payment ben gretely damaged whiche case h lden recompense theym thyrde poynt synner ought take hede confessyon entyer leuynge nothynge wyttynge defaute doo hym hath ben sayd dooth deuoyre flagelyte humayne soo defaute forgoten one many synnes whiche ought confesse partyculer confessyon hole poynt make grete doubte confessyon whiche theyr defaute take hede vnto comaundementes god accoplysshe kepe hy synne also hym accuse cofesse transgressyon whiche myght haue lerned vnderstonde one daye tweyne well suffycyently confesse euer theyr lyfe clerely vnderstonde peryll defaute man may consyder ye persone whiche xxx yere hath v c thre score sodayes whiche hath ben defended erthely werkes hym may lette thynke god benefyces thanke hym also ought lerne thynges necessary vnto soule thynke conscyence synnes confesse hym worthely moche grete party bodely people done yll theyr deuoure sondayes th e othe feestes thynke theyr coscyences confessed generall sholde co fessed partyculer yf holde theyr defaute nowe wryten well ryght reaso none ought haue prouffyte cryme defaute therfore excedeth myn vnderstandynge reason yf suche confessyons ben vylable god whiche thynge leue depnesses jugementes dyuyne fourth poynt synner ought take hede tell wherof hath mynde vnto one confessour vnto tweyne vnto many yf vnto wytrynge one parte vnto one parte vnto another malycyouslly synneth mortally shall assoyled one ne yf ony case sent agayne vnto souerayne shall suffyce tell case wherfore hath ben sent agayne hath tolde vnto fyrst fyfth poynt ought aduysed parfytly yf redy pardon good herte yll wyll vnto yt haue hym offended sayth oure sauyour euangelyste yf pardon vnto oure malefactours rancour haue agayn god shal pardon v lyke wyse hath offended ony persone worde dede oughte requyre pardon dede yf present ferme purpose place tyme whan shall fynde oportunyte vi poynt vnto regarde people whyche ben maryage two poyntes fyrst haue receyued sacrament maryage seconde maner ben gouerned vnto fyrst knowe ordenauce holy chirche none may take maryage kynnesman kynneswoman one party leest fyght degre whiche degree broder syster make ye fyrst chyldern whiche ben germays make seconde chylder germays whiche ben called remoued maketh thyrde chyldern remoued maketh iiii remoued remoued maketh fyfth sayd fyfth may haue maryage seconde thyrde fourth consequently lyne colla erall neuer may ony haue maryage hym whiche ryght lyne assendynge dyscendynge yf ony maryed wyttyngly wyth ony lygnage vnder degree sayd synneth mortally ouer acursyd noted habycyon carnall fornycacyon caus affynyte lynage well one parte degre whiche appertayne vn whiche comytten suche fornycacyon example thou co nyt test fornycacyon woma hyr systers naturalles ben thy systers affynyte neces ben thy neces germayns ben thy germayns lyke thynge woman regarde fornycatour may neuer mary frendes one ne yf mary wyttyngly ben acursyd ought departed notwithstondynge ony space tyme soo euer lyne comen suche maryage another thynge sholde yf maryage legytyme haue company carnall woman kynred husbonde husbonde kynred wyfe maryage shall departed partye culpable falleth suche inconuenyent may neuer requyre deuoyr maryage vnto partye yf fyrst dyspenced auctoryte pope synne mortally party whiche culpable hym ought yelde dyspleasaunce whiche may fall suche case partye culpable synneth mortally yf haue dysordynauce good counseyll suche persone conspable suche dyspensacyon pope eschew perylles whiche may come cause suche lettynge also ought take hede vnto lygnage spyrytuall whiche cometh amonge many persones cause sacrament baptem confyrmacyon knowe bytwene chylde baptysed whiche holden bytwene chyldern naturall ben borne sone doughter ony persone may neuer maryed marye chyldern naturalles theyr godfader godmoder godfaders godmoders well may mary theyr chyldern togyder whome gossypred comen many case may haue cause cognacyon legall affynyte yt men call justyce dyshoneste openly whiche passe cause shortnes also man ought mary begynnynge aduent tyll vnto ye vtas epephanie also septuagesime tyll vnto vtas ester also ye thre day ye assencyon tyll vnto vtas pentecost yt dooth wyse without dyspensacyon synneth mortallly vnto fyrst poynt sacrament maryage phere foloweth examynacyon persone maryed vnto seconde poynt whiche gouernynge persone maryed regarde sacrament maryage vnderstonde doctours declaren werke maryage may accomplysshed fyue maners tyme merytoryously somtyme synne somtyme synne venyall somtyme suche cyrcustaunces theologyens doubten mortall venyall somtyme mortall synne fyrst werke maryage may acco plysshed merytoryously whan ye one ye partyes ii togyder ben ye estate grace theyr intencyo haue lyne yelde ye maryage ye one eschewe peryll auoutry hym partye kepynge cyrcu staunces whiche appertayne vnto honeste maryage whan synne doute mortall venyall good suffycyent confessour may comprehende cyrcustaunces dede intencyon confessyon people maryed seuen maners man may synne mortally party declaren doctours fyrst suche whan man also ye woman ben moche dysordynate wyllen delyberacyon accomplysshe werke maryage party whiche maryage case harde juge vnto iugement humayn god whiche juge conscyence seeth clerely troweth seconde case whiche daunger synne mortal whan one partye refuseth withoute excusacyon lefull thyrde case whan ye man abused partye seche greter pleasure carnall fourth whan woman dyspocysyon body sholde yelde deuoyre maryage partye whiche hath knowlege moche vnresonable wyll hym abstayn synneth mortally sayen comenly doctours woman whiche obeyeth agayne wyll eschewe daungers incontynence yl le whiche may come maryage synneth fyfth whan people maryed goo vnto theyr wyues grete festes sayen doctours saynt thomas sayeth synne mortall deuoute doctour bonauenture also doctour subtyle scotte holden opynyon chirche defendeth werke maryage feestes alonely counseylleth man absteyn hym ende better dysposed praye vnto god moche man putteth herte pleasure carnalles moche man lesse dysposed praye vnto god ferther fro loue ought make suche abstynence comen assent lyke wyse techeth saynt poul yf one sayd partyes wyll absteyne partye ought obe ye without fermynge conscyence erronyous yf partye beleueth dedely synne obeye partye dede maryage tyme grete solempnyte neuerthelesse notwithstandynge hym obeyeth synneth mortally alonely moche dooth contrary conscyence whiche erronyous byleue obeye partye sayd tyme dedely synne vi whan werke maryage commytted place halowed chirche chirchyerde yf partyes maryed may otherwyse company togyders yf case knowen chirche chirchyarde sholde reconsyled ryght seuenth whan woman chylde nere tyme haue experyence true semblable chylde may renne ony peryll neuerthelesse theyr incontynence dyspose vnto suche pareyl synnen mortally doctours vn purpose haue founde tymes man maryed sorowe remors conscyence sought remedy counseyll wyfe hath hadde foure fyue chyldern deed fayr grete well formed whiche knowe cause ne ye occasyon ye dethe sayd chyldern cause coude juge vnder jugement god theyr incontynence sayd absteyn ony dysposycyon nerenesse chyldynge party appereth many maners estate honeste maryage euyll kept many people vyle carnall whiche oftymes comytten case bysshop many wronges make ony conscyence make ony confessyon oftymes god ponyssheth theyr lyue moche begete chyldern wronge croked lame blynde messelles fallynge grete yll sayen holy doctours therfore man sholde take hede teche yo ge people honoure reuerence fere obedyence ought kepe ye sacrament maryage sholde mary pryncypally entencyon haue lyne whiche may come vnto holy seruyce god holy chirche ye example yonge thobye vnto whome angell god taught wel wyfe sarra sholde absteyne ye dede maryage theyr benedyccyon espace thre dayes thre nyghtes whiche tyme sholde gyue vnto holy orysons dyde whiche delyuered al pareyll temptacyon deuyll whiche hadde strangled seuen husbondes whiche hadde espousyd one sayd sara alonely loue lyne sacrament maryage beaute ye doughter accomplysshe theyr pleasure carnalles doctryne techynge haue kepte syns many good crysten men well taught whome ben founde greate benediccion good lyne joye consolacyon longe lyfe seuenth poynt confessyon merytoryous suffycyent aske newly grace god whan done pryncypally custome fere worldely pryncypally loue god saluacyon ye soule whiche thynge done moost comenly may comprehended arguyde lyfe parte whiche grete payne represent one tyme yere ryght late theyr confessoure viii poynt whan sy ner hath wyll ferme purpose ceas put ende synne tyme come fle occasyons mortall synne ix wha synner cheseth vnto wyttynge confessour symple chapelayne whiche suffycyent idoniu redresse dede co scyence vocacyon estate whyche synner may whiche hath power assoyle x whanne synner hathe forgoten neclygence penaunce enioyned elles wyll requyre pardonne pardon restore another faste make prayer suche case confessyon none ought withdrawen good counseyll man accomplysshe hys penaunce estate grace soo doynge se heth grete meryte agayne god man acquyteth hym temporall payne p foloweth practyse ought holde whiche entyerly hym wyll confesse examen order x commaundementes lawe mooste sure maner may founde euer wyll well parfaytly exame caplm xiiii conscyence partyculer ought rule hym x commaundementes lawe wytnesseth saynt austen man may fynde certayne practyse examen well conscyence also sayth well saynt gregorye x commaundementes ben ten myrrours whiche soule crystened may clerely see knowe fylth synne dysordynaunce conscyence also sayth ryall prophete dauyd shall confesse well ryghtly moche haue lerned ten commaudementes god whiche well noted persone bounde hym confesse regulerly necessyte onely dedely synne whiche thynge transgressyon ony x comaundementes whiche ben defended seuen deedly synnes also conteyned seuen werkes mercy trouth artycles oure holy fayth whiche thynges vnderstonde commaundementes lawe artycles fayth seuen werkes mercy comprehended coteyned dede conscyence lyke wyse hath ben sayd therfore euer wyll hym well examen make parfyte hole confessyon thynges sayd ought take hede hath kepte acco plysshed ten comaundementes god well thynge comaunded sechynge vertues accomplysshynge werkes mercy also thynge defended ben seuen dedely synnes know pryde enuy wrath couetyse glotonye slouth lechery whiche seuen maner synnes man may falle often mortally dampnably somtyme venyall alonely byleue euery passyon mouynge ire enuy vayne glorye soo synnes sayd ben alwayes deedly synne whan suche passyons wylles abyden termes venyall synne exceden tyll vnto mortall synne thynge ryght harde vnto jugement humayne possyble therin gyue rule generall suffycyent juge euery case inpartyculer wheder mortall venyall hath ben sayd seuenth chapytre partye therfore nowe reste see partyculer case ordre ten comaundementes phere foloweth fyrste commaundement ouer thynges sayd fyrste comaundement caplm xv whiche wyll well purge co scyence ought take hede vnto poyntes folowen fyrste vnto brekynge vowes yf ony haue ben broken sayth carynge dyspysynge inobedyence agayne god whiche lawfull holde accomplysshe dedely synne yf man comytte suche fraccy delyberacyon equyualente rule put chapytre scyence confessour ought haue whiche oughte well noted case whiche folowen mater ten commaundementes also noted moche hath ben made mencyon treatyse comaundemen te seuen deedly synnes whiche studye boke wyll examen conseyence ought truste thynges whiche hath ben sayd generall especyall folowen recapitulacy comaundementes partyculer yf ony syknes forgetfulnes cause excusable breketh hys vowe synne alonely venyall yf hath auowed thynge vnlefull ne sholde accomplysshe without dyspense ought sooner contrary hym confesse soo folysshely haue auowed thynge whiche lefull honeste yf haue taryed accomplysshe vowes suche wyse hath forgoten moche taryenge falleth suche inconuenyent ne may accomplysshe grete theologyens wyll saye susteyne yt deedly synne yf haue made auowe faste thynge lefull ony cursyd ende come comytte thefte auoutry synne hath synned mortally yf hath made auowe chastyte relegyon afterwarde hym maryeth deedly synne many tymes often requyreth partye deuoure maryage synneth mortally yf requyred may acquyte hym yeldynge deuoyre maryage without deedly synne suche wyse loueth better wyll reason hym content accomplysshe werke maryage whiche thynge yl kepe tyme lyfe therfore yt ben suche inconuenyent sholde make dyspense theyr vowe assoyled synne noted curate may assoyle subiecte brekynge vowes may dyspence chaunge without specyall lycence pope bysshop case requyreth dyspensacyon comutacyon vowe chastyte pylgrymage vnto jherusalem rome saynt james ben reserued pope dyspence commutacyons vowes appertayne vnto prelate also noted yonge people knowe ye doughter vnder yeres xii accomplysshed sone vnder yeres xiiii may vowe entre relegyon theyr owne auctoryte withstondynge dyscrecyon euer may haue also auowe oblygatory yf made delyberacyon full consent also woman maryed may vowe obserue vowe yt hath made maryage yf husbond wyll consent yf hath auowed maryage husbonde may make leue without dyspense withoute synne ye one yf husbonde ony tyme consentynge man may well vowe without lycence partye whiche vnto preiudyce maryage also whiche vowen neuer kembe fryday spynne satyrdaye semblables superstytucyons ought leue suche vowes symple full vanytees doo ordenaunce theyr wyse dyscrete confessour holy faders secondly synner oughte well take hede yf culpable sorceryes wytchcraftes charmes inuocacyons deuyll adoracyons paccyon hym dyabolykes also yf yt haue vsed ony euyll crafte yf haue kepte retayned bokes also yf haue jugyd deth lyfe aduentures ony persone constellacyons knowlege planettes skye phylosephye also yf haue vsed sorte knowe ony thynge yf hath byleued ouer moche stedfastly aduentures ony dremes yf hath lokyd causyd loke token hande knowe aduentures hymself yf ony syknes hath vsed lytell scrowes charmes yf hath put dystyncyon certayne dayes tewesdaye wenysdaye dayes begynne ony werke make waye beleuynge one daye shall profyte better nother yf hath put fayth ony aduentures songe cryes ony byrdes metynge ony beestes thynges case sayd oftymes dedely synne ryght selden venyall synne phere foloweth seconde commaundement thynges sayd seconde caplm xvi commaundement synner onght take hede vnto poyntes whiche folowen yf hath sworne certayne thynge whiche doubte mortall synne specyally jugemente yf hath sworne thynge whiche selfe yll sholde synne hath synned mortally suche othe ought kepte accomplysshed yf hath shewed wyttyngly secrete counseyll hath sworne holde secrete dedely synne well hym swereth hym whiche wyttyngly maketh suche reuelacyon knowynge well gyuen hym kepe secrete yf hath sworne detestably ye blode yt deth wombe lorde dedely synne suche maner swere reputyd also blaspheme lyke wyse dysplease ire god sayntes yf hath promysed sworne ony thynge lefull trespasseth without excusary resonable vnto wyttynge dedely synne thynge sworne may suche te chylde thynge semblable whiche accomplysshed synne venyall yf hath constrayned hym swere byleueth shall forsworne deedly synne except iuge whiche order ryghte maketh swere ony justice yf songes vnhoneste tryfylles talkynges langage swereth god sayntes deedly synne also swere troweth cause thynge also euery worde may grete payne done without contenement lawe god consequent deedly synne phere foloweth thyrde commaundement thynges spoken thyrde commaundement caplm v synner ought take hede vnto poyntes whiche folowen yf occupy hymselfe seruantes chyldern worldly werkes cursyd sonday festes gyuen commaundement couetousnes without constraynt necessyte dedely synne well hym commaundeth hym whiche obeyth consenteth yf hath gone vnto fayres vnto markettes couetousnesse sayd feestes may synne mortally thynge shall masse herde yf may goodly gooth vnto fayrres vnto markettes prelate holy chirche suffren without makynge specyall prohybycyo without makynge ony punysshement yf occupyed daye dysportes feestynges goynge huntynge hawkynge herynge masse somtyme occupye se deedly synne comenly sholde take hede seche good counseyll tauerners baker hocsters potycaryes bayllyues lyke wyse sergeautes offycers also tayllers cordyners generally maner people labour noblesse euer degree ben euery man hym ought examen vocacyon estate whiche lyueth take hede occasyon cyrcumstaunces yf occupyed holydaye worldly werkes yf hath ben pryncypally couetousnes dedely synne also frawdes euyll thoughtes clamacyons pariurynges tryfylles whiche oftymes comytten maner marchaudyse weyght mesure pryce substauce qualyte greuous synne holydaye sholde another daye moche doynge transgressyon comaundementes yt thyrde whiche halowe feestes whiche pryncypally werke synne also seuenth whiche defendeth thefte shall sayd phere foloweth fourth commaundement thynges sayd fourth comaudement caplm xviii synner ought take hede vnto poyntes folowen fyrst yf hath spoken wordes vnlefull vnto fader vnto moder yf hath cursyd yf hath mockyd yf hath put stryken yf theym hath prouoked wrathe wronge dedely synne yf theym wolde obeye thynge whiche good lawfull deedly synne whan contempt another thynge sholde yf ouer syght ony neclygence thynge lytell reputacyon yf ne hath purueyde theyr necessytes may ought yf vnto borne honoure reuerence place tyme comenly dedely synne yf hath acquyte theyr deth accomplysshe theyr laste wylles testamentes may ought well deedly synne yf hath ben irreuerende vnto frendes vnto souerayns vnto people chirche vnto offycers vnto lordes yf hath taught chyldern houshold makynge kepe comaundementes god receyue sacramentes place tyme prouydynge meete drynke clothe hosynge honestly power hys estate yf hath causyd leue pryde bosty ge vanytes yf hath suffred fou de dauces companyes peryllous vnhoneste yf hath made seruant seruantes werke holydayes thynges e may haue deedly synne cyrcumstaunces modyfycacyon mortall synne whiche hath ben spoken tofore phere foloweth fyfth commaundement thynges sayd fyfth caplm xix commaundement synner ought take hede vnto poyntes folowen fyrste yf hath done manslawghter ony persone dede thought yll doynge vsynge thynges vnlefull sholde caste stone without dyscrecyon ny draught doynge thynge vnleful aduyseth whiche may dau ger necessyte euytable whiche necessyte sholde fallen culpe yf hymself defendyng kylleth husbonde ony woman whome sholde foude vnhonestly case dedely synne also yf ony iuge gyue sentence deth enuy ire couetousnes vpon whiche hath deserued dye deedly synne yf woman chylde take ony thynge procure dethe fruyte whiche counseyllynge therto consenten synnen mortally folowe dede deth ye chylde yf ye fruyte hath soule sholde homycyde case bysshop whiche gynen couseyll consentyng aydynge yf fader moder nouryce stop breth lytyll chylde ouersyght otherwyse may deedly synne theyr neclygece defaute good kepynge yf woman chylde moche laboure auaryce holde acquaynted daunce ordynaunces leseth hyr fruyte synneth mortally yf ony smyte shoue woman chylde suche jurysdyccyon leseth fruyte dedely synne yf manor woman enforce fynde wayes maners whiche may lette ye woman conceyue chylde deedly synne yf ony smyte hurte takynge hy ony membres vsage order justyce deedly synne yf gyue counseyll comaundement ratifye hath excepte ony kylled beten agayne ye ordre justice charyte deedly synne withstandynge dede folowe yf desyre deth nother delyberacyon hate enuy ony cursyd cause deedly synne another thynge sholde desyre deth ony malefactours moche hurte goodes ony good man jugement humayne yf smyte wounde wrongefully ony chirche chirchyarde sacrylege place halowed polutyde yf hath made make causeth made justes whiche may peryll deth synne many case partyculers may come touchynge mater fyfth commaundement whiche vnto whome comen ought aduyse pourge foloweth vi commaundement thynges sayd vi commaundement caplm xx whiche suffycyently ynoughe hath ben spoken dyuers maners lechery synner sholde take hede vnto poyntes whiche folowen fyrste yf hath touched vnhonestly kyssed drawe persone vnto synne lechery deedly synne notwithstandy ge none thynge folowe yf hath wryten borne sente letter vnto knowlege prouoke ony persone vnto synne lechery deedly synne yf hath made songes spoken herde whiche sholde vyle prouokynge vnto synne lechery pryncypally enduce hym vnto synne deedly synne yf hath accompanyed ony yf hath gyuen fauoure assembles yf hath made message presentes drawe vnto synne lechery deedly synne lyke wyse whiche vnto suche intencyon receyuen gyftes promysses yf hath taken delectacyon thynke dede lechery whiche deedly synne synneth mortally whan delyberacyon yf hath hadde cursyd wyll consented vnto dede lechery suche wyll proceden lokynges spekynges touchynges hym deely synne lyke wyse wyll wherof suche thynges proceden suche wyll dede foloweth ben two synnes ben one alonely ought full well take hede euery good persone hys prayer lokes abyllymentes ne gyueth occasyon vnto another folysshe thought cursyd wyll occasyon may suche yt sholde dedely synne also noted synne lechery proceden many passyons meane whome man falleth oftymes vnto synne grete inconuenyens knowe offuscacyon knowlege vnderstandynge preceptacyon incosyderacyon inconscyence loue dysordynate owne sensualyte loue present lyfe hate ye justyce ordenau ce god therfore synner ought exame yf synne lechery suche wyse occupyed hath lefte thynke god hys saluacyon yf hath ben precypytant without delyberacyon werkes besynes yf hath ben without due examynacyon hath done yf hath chauged good purpose hath lefte aboue doo yf hath excessyuely sought pleasure case hys body yf hath moche loued present lyfe delytes flesshe yf hadde dyspleasure lawe god moche defendeth concupyscence worlde flesshe euery thynges haue grete exces deedly synne declareth saynt gregorye phere foloweth seuenth commaundement thynges sayd seuenth comaundement vnto synne couetyse ye synner sholde take hede vnto poyntes folowen fyrste symony seconde vsury thyrde fraudes decepcyons fourth iniquyte agayne justyce fyfth bysshoppes syxte chanons quam magi cipale non minus pricipal knowe ye syluer may self ende pryncypall make prayer predycacyo prayer made intencyon pryncypally haue syluer put vnto folysshe vsages deedly synne symony sacrylege lyke vnto synne juda vnto regarde masse whiche taken xii pen whiche ben worth thyrty pen put folysshe vsage may wexe ryche auaryce maners indeuyde yf sayd prayer made bymag io gerso synners thynges soo moche lesse worth knowe ye agayne thew whiche make suche preestes synge wyttyngly yf hath renou cyd vnto ony benefyce suche paccyon yt sholde gyuen vnto kynnysman vnto ony whiche doynge hym hath promysed ony thynge temporall symony one mo many case symonye may founde well prelate chirche lordes temporall degree persones whome passe ouer tyme cause shortnes notwithstondynge clerke well aduysed whiche receyuynge ordres benefyces fallen symony irreguler synneth mortally executynge offyces holy ordres dyspensyd p foloweth vsury whiche comyttyd well dede wyll vnto seconde whiche vsurers synner ought take hede yf hath le te money thynge wherof vsage consumpcyon sholde corne wyne paccyon intencyon pryncypall receyue gaue vsury deedly synne yf hath lente vpon gage thynge moeuable also herytage suche condycyon pryncypall intencyon shall haue vsage fruytes leue sayd charge without deductynge rebaytynge somme lente vsury excepte gendred kynnysman whiche taketh ony wage attendynge promysse whiche vnto hym hath ben made cause maryage wyfe suche wyse mayntene husbonde ought mayntene espouse well notyd mater ben two maners vsuryes one clerely open sayd hyd commytte dyuers maners yf hath bought londes possessyons lytyll mynyssheth pryce moche seller putteth bargayne may bye agayne herytage wt certayne tyme comytteth vsurye yf rebate hath receyued ouer costes layenges ye sayd herytage yf sell many tymes harder leneth abaytynge payment tyll vnto certayne tyme may sewe specyally whan loueth better haue vpon ower lesse pryce tarye also whan hath bought certay ware corne wyne whiche ben yet gadre moche hath auauncyd yc payment gyueth lesse thynge worthe ower tyme sholde receyue vsery also whan leneth pryncypally intencyon haue presentes money ayde thynge temporall vsurye yf hath betaken bestyall vnto haluys suche condycyon yt yf happen mortallyte aduenture losse wherof whiche taken cause neuertheles catyll shal euer sauf entyer vsury rewle generall alwayes suche contractys shepe la be hyre ox bestes one partyes maketh pryce paccyon suche maner assured wynne nothynge lese euer happen partye abydeth doubte subiecte aduentures fortune suche cotracte agayn reason agayne justyce whan exces one partye suche greate payne may losse gayns soo yt entende fraude one vnto put euery awayte vnto owne proffyte none vsurye yf procurer tuter ony faderles chyldern gyueth theyr fynauce vnto vsury ende yt sayd fynauce vnto shall prouffyte meane nourysshed theyr maryages augmented also poore marchaundes suche meane myght auantage notwithstondynge sholde deedly synne sayd procuroure tutour bounde restore sayd vsurye case yf whiche haue hadde prouffyte wyll restore lyke wyse ben pryncypally bounde also well noted yt many seller byers ben full vsurye god good conscyence well cause entencyon beynge also sellynge whiche alwayes semen lawfully solde forme contracte wordes example martyn hath necessyte fynde hundreth crownes lene seynge knowynge man hym wyll pleasur cometh vnto petyr vnto hym wynge necessyte whiche dysposed selle hym xl shelynges rente vpon herytage suche condycyon tyll vnto terme seuen yeres many tymes often shall yelde somme lent hundreth crownes peter hounde hym delyuer herytage suche case semblables intencyon condycy ons seller byer sholde weyed consydered yf seller hadde intencyon yt xl shelynges sholde abyde euer vnto byer whiche entencyon ye byer knoweth vnto hym semblable meane also party wylled desyred contracte made vnder forme sale wynnynge vnto without knowlege vsury hundreth crownes may purchase vpon hym suche contracte especyall god malycyous auaryce erthely people hath many founde eauil lacyons grete payne may go waye moost gretest moost yllumyned doctours whiche cause passe ouer fro case partyculers also holden manifeste fourthly vnto contrarye laste case vnderstande puttynge gayn certayne chatell vnder incertayne example lene hondreth crownes wher thou shalte marchaundyse pareyll somme suche wyse yere another erme thou shall yelde syx crownes x mo lesse yf thou lese fortune sayd hondreth crownes vpon al yf sauyd shall yelde somme spoken suche contracte full vsury ryghte cause suche hope suche lener hath wynne lese fyfthly puttynge gayn chatell certayne example lene hundreth crownes suche wyse yere paste thou shalte yelde hondreth x vsury manyfeste vnto v maner lene may broughte ouer doctours make questyon yfa questyon lawfull ony case receyue ony thynge lone lawfull fyue manersthe answ fyrst man may well receyue thynge spyrytual lone good grace hym vnto whome hath lente also yf free wyll gyueth ony thynge may receyue lone hath made suche intencyon secondely reason dysdamage yf lone hath ben made vnder certayne payne yelde certayne tyme defaute lender dammage without ficcyon caas may cause dysdamage take sayd payne pryncypall yf sayd payne excessyue vnreasonable thyrdely reason cause doubte vnto whiche lender submysed lyke wyse appyreth seconde caas notable sayd lendynge vnto halfe losse gayns fourthely reason dammage renneth whiche lended cause sayd redy example grete request lende hondred crownes yere whiche god good conscyence shall dammage somme ten twenty crownes yf whiche borowed seeth sholde better vnto prouffyte take sayd somme restore damage lendynge may receyue ouer pryncypall kepe hym recompense hym damage fyfthtly reason hyre thynge whiche may hyre ox horse thynges man may receyue tymes valour tyme hyre hyre receyue man hath lente ony maner wyse hath ben sayd done ayenst comaundement man selleth thynge imprecyable whiche proprely may solde vnderstande pleasure charyte euery creature ought vnto neyghbour well ye lawe nature lawe holy scrypture whiche lawes ben canon cyuyles defenden ye synne vsurye also yf ony gyne olde corne thynge semblable renewe hauynge intencyon pryncypall newe shall worth elles wolde gyue comytted vsurye yf pryncypally intente thynge perysshe pleasure vnto neyghbour trewe semblable doubte yf thynge worthy lesse tyme shall yelded agayne suche caas none vsurye payne vsurers publysshed suche ben excomunycate ryght wherfore holy chirche defended vnto suche gyuen precyous body jhesu cryste also theyr oblacyon receyued holy chirche also theyr deth theyr bodyes ben cast voyde grounde receyued place holy blessyd man ought doubte soules theym whiche deyen suche estate ben dampned deuylles helle wherfore bodyes sholde put reste faythfull crysten men yf theyr laste dayes requyre penaunce may assoyled doynge yt yt possyble restore vsuryes yt haue receyued theyr lyf suffysed receyued vnto ye sacrament holy chirche assoyled orden theyr testament yt theyr dethes vsuryes ben restored behoued dyspose mouable herytage tyll vnto ye somme whiche may amoute sayd vsuryes yf vnto whome ought make restytucon ben present hy behoued make full satysfaccion yeldynge fynauce maruell gage assygnacon yf ben absent ye juge ye court lyuetenaut ye bysshop deane curate sholden represent ye persones suffycyent restytucyon satysfaccyon ought restored yf possyble oonly somme hath ben receyued vsurye damage myght haue hadde cause theym whiche haue payed sayd vsuryes whiche apyreth clerely full fewe vsurers escapen deuyll lyke wyse also appyreth peryll whiche receyuen theyr chirches chircheyerdes vnto sepulture body vsurer suche hath ben spoken preestes whiche wyttyngly ben excomunycate ipso vsurye whiche hath accustomed synne moche greuous shortely vnto seconde poynt p foloweth fraude decepcyon vnto thyrde poynt whiche fraudes decepcyons whiche comytted dyuers maners people dyuers maners synner sholde take hede fyrste dede marchaundyse ouer thynges sayd vsurye yf hath done fraude fals weyghtes ony fals mesures sellynge ony fals thynge corrupte meddled affermynge good pure metalles appotecaryes wyne oyle ony ware whiche byer notably defrauded deedly synne syns lytell thynge venyall synne well noted yf ony man defraude dysceyued neyghbour lytell thynge hym wolde well dysceyue seygnourye justyce haue made prestes tax imposicyons auaryce tyrannye comen wele mortall synne also yf hath falsed bookes receyte lettres vnto notable damage deedly synne also yf marchaut marchaudyse pryncypally auaryce encrease catell lyue honestly vocacyon ayde poore welth comunalte deedly synne whan suche gayns putteth pryncypall entente yf ony bye stuffe ware intencyon selle agayne derer without chaungynge doynge ony crafte corne wyne sholde waye wryte wood make ony crafte selle without caryenge one regyon comon welth pryncypally secheth suche maner encrease catell suche marchaundyse vnlawfull may haue deedly synne sayth mayster frauces de maronis also yf haue made paccyon bytwene selle theyr ware rudely pryce competent whiche comons constayned bye theyr pryce deedly synne also yf payed one ware whiche seynge hath aboue made owne mynysseth hurteth mortally deedly synne also yf hath payed symple people fals moneye fraude decepcyon deedly synne also yf hath vsed flaterynge speche ye amouted ende yere yt man hath made cc suche journey ye somme xvi viij whiche somme ought make restitucyon oftyme happened jugement god yt vnto suche people theyr goodes encrease yet profyten dyspende tauernes vnto cometh loss damage ye whiche fallen necessyte pouerte power restore yt whiche sholde wel reason suche meane ben deceyued deuyll without nombre ayded confessours ignorauntes whiche assoylen su che people without enioynynge restytucyon without counsyll whiche vpon sholde gyuen p foloweth iniquyte defaute justyce vnto iiij poynt whiche iniquyte justyce yt defaute yelde justyce reason vnto neyghbour synner ought take hede moche yelde kepe defende justyce aperteyned pryncypally vnto prelate hol chirche vnto ye lordes erthely ye jurisdiccon euery extended consequetly vnto juges aduocat proctours notaryes sergeautes prentyses wytnesses euery estate maners persones thynge ought shewed examen well fyrst prelacyon seygnoury ecclesyastycall yf irreguler suspende excomunycate bygame illegittinie cubinarie open knowen consequens suspende tyme houre yt receyued dygnyte cure prelacyon synned mortally contynually deedly syne executynge offyce comytted alwayes newe deedly synne ye dyspence absolucon yf hath ben elect canonly college patrone vnto whome apperteyned hath receyued confermed hym yt hath power vnto yt come meanes forboden suche called ye ryght wronge doer theef yf hath ony maner puyssaunce jurysdyccyon dyspose make offyce ony thynge temporall spyrytuall aperteynynge vnto offyce benefyce synned mortally oftentymes hym endeuoured excecute whiche aperteyned vnto sayd offyce benefyce yf hath made prayer hymselfe chosen receyued vnto sayd offyce symonyacle yf hath paccyon couenaut dyspence aperteyned vnto ye pope dyspence holdeth theuyshly offyce dygnyte yf suffre dyssymule ony grete ylle subgectes may ryght purge correcte deedly synne yf hath fauoured ony ayenst justyce vnto damage yf hath lost wasted goodes ye chirche folysshe vsages yf hath rebelled ayenst reason vnto soueraynes also yf hath ben neclygent gete good suffycyent counseyll seche justyce whiche defaute partye hath ben damage thynges dedely synne also yf hath put offycers indygne vnworthy specyally cure soules man knoweth suche may wtsaye lawfully repelle neclygent deedly synne also yf hath suffred confessours ignorau te grete peryll damage soules whiche may vndertake deedly synne indygne moche ignoraut apyreth chapytre scyence necessarye vnto confessour also yf hath ben curyous proude buyldynges heyght horse harneys abyllyment grete peryllous dyspences vnto grete damage well chirche poore deedly synne also yf hath ben curyous temporalyte spyrytualyte exces moche lytell mortall synne venyall also yf hath lefte lese ryght preuyleges prelacyon benefyce aperteynen ryght neclygence may mortall also yf hath dyspensed vndyscretely whiche become recheles vnthryfty contrarye haue ben harde inhumayne dyspense puru ye enfermetes subgectes exces moche lytell mortal synne venyall also ought lyght example vnto subgectes thynges fewe wordes thynges prouffytable quenchynge dyscordes reprouynge detraccyons bac ytynge grutchynges fals reportes mockeryes hym behoued yelde acounte also correccyon whiche vnto hym apperteyned cause offyce ouer comune whiche ought lawe charyte whiche ben made mencyon also bou de pastoure shepe good shepeherde good doctryne good example defende vnto power wolues rauysshynge ben prechours prechen pryncypally go theyr syluer goodes also tyrautes extorcyoners whiche oftentymes deuouren vnto wyttynge knowledge prelate may haue suche exces neclygence circumstaunces mortall synne prelate spyrytuall ought fader defender poore people child faderles moderles also wydowes ought haue specyall herte theyr cause p behoued seche dispence yt execute theyr offyces hath gyuen holy ordres wyttyngly vnto yt haue age determyn ryght deedly synne may dyspence sayd tyme hath gyuen ordres wyttyngly vnto ony ye whiche hath sholde precede gyue ordres tyme ryght wtout ye dispence ye pope deedly synne whiche hath ben ordeyned supende hath lefte ony thynge saye whiche essence sacrament holy ordres hym behoued go backe moche suche sacrament create god gyueth token spyrytuall named caractere thynge sholde yf lefte thynge whiche sholde essencyall man sholde supplye ordres yt whiche forgoten hagynge clerke ordened shol hath receyued vnto holy ordres without tytle suffysaut hath vysyted dyocyse ryght reason ryquyred prouydynge confessours mynysters correctynge defautes whiche done ayenst sacramentes offyce dyuyne grete noy e also drynkynges etynges done chirche place halowed synned greuously hath fou de gyuen noualtees relykes hath denouced vnto people auaryce pryncypally yf hath extorcyoned cautell fayre excomunycate lykewyse apyred ye clementyne also yf hath receyued vnto sepulture ye whiche seeth eche torment defended syned mortally concubynarye open knowen yt yt lawfully vaynquysshed yt hath yt confessyd jugement yt synne open euydent yt parysshe grete partye knowed yt grete perseuerauce yt noman ought doubte suspende vnto hymselfe vnto yf saye masse admynyster sa ramet suche estate irreguler sayth ostyense moreouer lawyer holden yt suche case may dyspence alonely ye auctoryte holy syege apostolycall opynyon holden rycharde de medium villa scotte john andrewe astence panorme thynge stolen cause sayd theft also yf suche thynge stolen perysshe fortune ellys yf abyde alwayes whiche hath stolen bounde yf hath done deuoyre offre restytucyon thynge perysshe whiche restytucyon endamaged hath wyll receyue yf hath boughte wyttyngly thynge stolen rauysshed whiche wyse aperteyneth vnto seller hath intencyon bye retayne hym selfe ouer mortall synne holden restore vnto hym vnto whome apertayneth thynge bought vnto inherytours vnto poore hath ben sayd without power repute pryse hath gyuen onely vnto hym hym hath made suche sale also ouer holden kepe harmeles warande hym vnto whome appertayneth thynge stolen soo euer become yf boughte good intencyon knowe yelde vnto loste may justly repute somme gyuen yelde alonely surplus may worth yf fynde hym vnto whome suche thynge appertyneth yt surplus ought gyuen vnto pore yf hath bought thynge whiche hath ben stolen whiche byleueth loyalte holden restore tyll vnto certefyed trouth duely certefyed holden restore durynge tyme byleueth thynge loyalte peryssheth consumed parte bounde restore alonely party fruytes hath tyme byleued thynge solde truely also eten drynken rauen thefte holden restore vnto estymacyon haue taken excepte whiche ben grete necessyte vnto whome may semblable shall please well vnto whome ye sayd thynge rauysshed stolen appertayneth sholde prechers whiche entende enduce theuys amendement vnto restytucyon also wyse chyldren seruautes whiche haue theyr goodes thefte vsury symony rauen ben holde restore valour may haue sayd thefte drynke meete hose cloth otherwyse onely moche haue laboured take payne ammonycion wyse restytucyon made vnto partye also yf goodes whiche euyll goten hath whiche truely goten may adresse theyr intencyon lyue goodes thefte may lyue wt theyr laboure sholde demaude prouysyon justyce yf may lyue ony wayes sayd sholde sooner demau de almes lyue thefte alonely case extreme necessyte also ignorauce may excuse moche persones sayd also ye poore whiche receyuen demauden almes si inuenisti et eddidisti rapu hee aug habetur lx q v also yf haue founde ony thynge whiche appertayneth vnto nother comytteth thefte reteynyug heuysshely agayne reason agayn good wyll ordeyned hym vnto whome suche thynge may appertayne therfore yf know vnto whome appertayneth ought make cryed open place yf partye founde taryenge suffycyent ought departyd vnto poore good dyscrecyon fynder may abyde longe tyme gode prompte conscyence restore oftymes many partye shall foude another thy ge shall thynges founde whiche hath tymes possessyon domynacyon ony persone fyndeth may retayne ony place yf sholde olde auncyent tresours foude ye herytage another lawe cyuyle halfe apertayneth vnto lorde herytage parte vnto hym whiche hath founde vnto thats e est regnu celoru thesauro abscondito agro que uenit ho abscodit et p gandio vadit dit vniuersa q h e e agru illum math xiii qd furto subla est me fura attenditur ix vi ca v item deusno iudicat ex oib sed ex cogi acoibus xxii q ii x q v non sane ite tho ii li extra de exco li vi ca caueant sane abinuito sumit iniuriose affert na pleri que ne mendico volut redde e honore suu nec oper rio mercede nec hec q ab inuito ccipiunt per iniu purpose semeth besayd parable euangelyste yf ony fynde tresoure felde goth byeth well herytage whiche tresoure hydde lorde tresoure well reason fou de reason possessyon herytage also fynder may poore may good counseyll prelate confessour retayne thynge founde specially whan knoweth vnto whome restore also thynge founde may lytell valoure man ought forme conscyence restore whan wyll shall suche man shall take wylfully grete thynge suche lytell thynge man byleueth iniury dysplesure vnto hym vnto whome appertayneth may haue mortall syne thorne nedyll nother lytell thynge wyll weyed god werke outwarde yf hath taken theuysshly godes hym whiche vnto hym oweth ony somme tyll vnto pryce dette lesse good coscyence consyderynge ouer well paye hym without plee lettynge maner yll synne fere god pacyence damage may purchase grete meryte neuertheles suche case holden bounde restore hym ouer sayen yf suche maner takynge theuysshely sentence excomunycate caste whiche hath taken sayd acursyd holy chirche intendeth bynde suche sentence witholdeth fro another agayne reason malycyously whiche thynge doth whiche payed sayd notwithstondynge lawe ciuyle sholde culpable punysshed foloweth falleth sayd sentence sholde take hede vnto whome suche case sholde come gyue doynge sclaunder euyll example vnto neyghbours yf offycer take gyftes seruyces pleser vnto ony vnto preiudyce justyce dammage another deedly synne also yf thretenynges otherwyse extorcyoneth gyftes promysses journey thynge notable ought restore payne pleasure done resonably may receyue vnto hym shall gyue lyberally lordes chirch secularyte may receyue amendes yt ben taxed theyr courtes ryght good custome soo done hate couetyse cursyd occasyon good counseyll departe suche amendes vnto power specyall whan amendes surmonteth damage yf hath vsyd wyttyngly thynge lent ouer termes wyll lener synneth mortally holden make satysfaccyon yf thynge lente impeyre loste holden restore yf hath lente wyttyngly ony thynge tonne musty put wyne horse another thynge whiche cometh damage vnto hym whiche borowed lener holden kepe hym harmeles also whiche hyred wynne journey ony werke ye whiche vndertaketh carye tone wyne voweth thynge holden restore da mages whiche cometh vnto sayd werke defaute notellys yf haue taken kepe ony thynge ought yelde excepte case fyrste whan shall yelde vnto grete yl damage hym vnto whome man sholde yelde sholde yelde glayue vnto man furyous seconde whan thefe hath gyuen kepe thefte man sholde yelde sooner vnto lorde thyrde whan gyuer sholde forfayte whiche goodes shold lyke wyse irreuerenter est opositum jurare sine causa et vtilicate est porcio irreuerecie veritatis diuine juracio nominis dei vbi nulla est necessitas vel vtilitas valde est irreprehensibilis juramentum incautum quod fit sine causa vel necessitate importat irreuerenciam diuini nominis non solum iuramentum mendax sed eciam quod fit sine necessitate et vtilitate est secundo precepto inibitum jurare sine causa est nomen dei vanu assumere disponit homine ad conceptu dei non est iurandum de falso nec de mutili et non eciam nisi de iusticia et veritate iuramentum debet esse discreta deliberacio vt non iuretur verum nisi pro necessitate vel vtilitate ex irreuerencia nascitur iurandi consuetudo que peccatum est iugens et mortale et non solu vnum sed multiplex consentus interpretauimus est quando quis negliget reprimere aliquod inductum est mortale contempus dei sine peccato mortali esse potest thynges sygnifyed conclusyons auctorytes well holy scrypture doctours sayd alleged appereth clerely multyplyenge reg anna loquebatur corde suo et vox penitus non audiebatur syxtly wt reuerece humylyte fere luce xviii publicanus non audebat leuare oculos suos ad celum seuenthly ought made secrete place pryue mathei vi tu aute cum oraueris intra cubiculu tum et clau ostio os patrem eyghtly poornes herte coscyence p iniquitate si aspexi corde meo exaudiet dns nynethly wt terys ye lost spirytuall cordyal audiui oracione tua vidi lacrimas tuas et ide tho tenthly wt attecyon vnto whiche man speketh demaudeth p intede voci oraconis mee rex meus de c ergo et tu attede enleuenthly wt grete feruour spyrite hie xlviii maledictus facit opus dei neglygenter tweluethly ought accompanyed wt gode holy werkes tho xii bona e oracio cu ieiunio et mathei v beati misericordes thyrtenthly wt perseuerauce daye daye fro good vnto better actum apostolierant perseuerantes cu mulieribus et maria matrem eius thynges sayd appereth necessyte noblesse prouffyte true oryson sayth john crisostum shall speke may pardon v reforme brynge true obseruauce blyssed co maudementes holy grace benedyccyon merytes oure lady gloryous moder blyssed sayntes oure poore soules yllumyne ye ende fynally may come vnto blyssed fruccyon amen p foloweth ryght prouffytable applicacyon arte phesecyan practyse ye whiche phesecyan spyrytuall ought holde interrogacyons man ought make vnto hym whiche artycle deth caplm xxvi seche conserue lyfe helth corporall many stodyen ryght desyrouslye well theorique practyser arte phesyke greter reason moche soule noble body lyfe glorye dygne teporall euery true crysten man sholde studye know eschewe synne whiche syknes soule cause deth eternall foloweth brefe recolleccyon arte physyke spyrytuall founded twelue rule scyence physyke corporall lyke wyse v techeth ryght gloryous apostle saynt poul meane manduccyon thynges corporalles sensybles man may come vnto contemplacyon spyrytualles therfore vnto v hath gyuen swete ihesu cryste true saumarytayn physycyans oursoules physyke holy sacramentes vnder forme thynges corporall fere answereth well syknes medecyne also syke body asmoche occasyon fyrst synne etynge apple whiche thynge corporall ihesu cryste vnto v hath gyuen precyous body ryght holy blood vnder semblaunce brede wyne baptysme sacramentes lyke wyse well agayne metynge synne orygenall vnto regarde physycyan ihesu cryste whiche god man togyders syke body man woman body materyall spyrytuall whiche good ryght appereth physyke corporall man may treate gyue vnderstonde spyrytuall fyrste rule physecyan ought vnderstonde helth syknes ellys may enduce one put lyke wyse ought physycyan spyrytuall vnderstonde confessour know synne whiche sykenes soule estate grace god whiche helth soule wherfore noted helth corporall isquatuor sut humores saguis tleuma colera melancolia good dysposycyon whiche cometh armony consyderacyon foure humour vnderstonde blode coler fleume malancoly whan foure kepe degree wtout excedynge hauynge rule ye coplexyon ye supposaut helth corporall contrary exces defaute tribulacyon ye one many ye sayd humour causeth syknes applycacyon lyke wyse whanquatuor passiones ira cocupisce cia timor tristicia foure pryncypall passyons soule vnderstonde ire concupyscence fere heuynes benduely ordeyned amodered soule well dysposed helth spyrytuall ye contrary whan ben dysordenate troubled syknes playnly vnderstonde mater know yt whan passyon ire vnto regarde thynges ye whiche may soner ye loue ye creatour whan cocupyscence desyre regarde goodes glory fere vnto ye regarde dapnacyon heuynes vnto regarde synnes whiche haue commyt soule well dysposed helth spyrytuall thanne contrary whan foure passyons ben dysordenate vnto regarde thynges erthely soule falleth langoure excessyue syknes seconde rule phesecyan ought enquyre cause helth atuor qualitates calor rigiditas siccitashumiditas syknesses euery thyge produceth bryngeth forth nouryssheth effecte whiche notyd whan foure qualytes tosu cecidit igniset viderut sole p lvii vnderstonde hete colde drye moystour ben certayne good porcyon vnto regarde suppost causen armonye helthtrepida ersit timore vbi erat timor p lii lyke wyse exces diminucyon perturba cyon one agayne ye causen syknes applycacyon lyke wyse vnto soule heinici sapietimor dni p cx te vnto v sygnyfyed loue whiche may well ordeyned agayne god dysordynate agayne thynges erthely causeth ye soule helth syknes lesse ordenaunce dysordenaunce colde sygnyfyed fere whiche may worldely humayne seriule vycyous causeth syknes spyrytuall may helth fylyale begynnyng true sapyence causeth helth drynes sygnyfyed heuynes whiche may dysordynate moche lytell moche heuy aduersytes worldly lytell offence dyshonour god moystnes sygnyfyeth delytes pleaser without whiche soule resonable may lyue yf ben worldely carnall causen syknes yf ben god thynges spyrytuall causen helth spyrytuall thyrde rule physycyan bygrego sicut arte medicie calida frigidis frigida calidiscuratur ita dns nt traria oppo medica ta pctis vt lubricis tineci tenacib largitate iracudis masue tudine elatis preciperet humilitate thyng contraryous sholde chase thother yf syknes hote ought gyue medycyne colde yf cause coldenes oughte gyue medycyne hete soo cause applycacyon lyke wyse physyke spyrytuall lyke wyse ihesu cryste techeth whiche saynt gregorye declareth agayne lechery man sholde put abstynauce drynke meete vsynge takynge hede agayn couetyse almesded agayne ire furour pacyence heuynes agayne pryde humylyte whiche maner remedy ought vnderstonde whan cause suffycyent wherfore resonably man sholde wyse fourth rule physycyan conseruenon solo pane vivit ho sed oi verbo qd procedit de ore dei deut viii mat iiii qui seuerauerit fine hic salu erit mat x quid pricipiis obsta sero medicina paratur cum mala logas ualuere mor mu tarept ethiopspel lem sua pardus varietatessuas e vospoteritisb sa cere sididisceritis malu hiero xiii c helth recoueryd whiche thyng done foure maners fyrste vsynge good meetes secondly takynge good drynke thyrdly eschewynge drynke excessyf noysaut fourthly holdynge hym good ayre lyke wyse vnto dede spyrytuall fyrste herynge good doctrynes predycacyons se condly desyre alwayes better worth thyrdly occupyenge hym holy operacyons forellys longe goynge man may eschewe euylles fourthly perseuerynge good werkes without perseuerauce good lyfe man may neuer come hyre rewarde fyfth rule physycyan dylyge ce remedye begynnynge syknesses greate payne thorne areched moche putteth rote depnes applycacyon lyke thynge synne hym wyll plante soule ire enuy pryde lechery synne wyll resyste begynnynge therto may come easely deffereth longe tyme wt grete payne therto cometh therfore sayth well holy scrypture hath blessynge god whiche casteth lytelnes yongth nourysshed whanne man requyreth ayde ihesu cryste whiche named true stone moche foundacyon holy fayth catholyque holy chirche syxte rule f phesycyan yt ought know tokenes sykenes whichenota quattuor signa ifirm ben foure fyrste whan persone hath loste apetyte seconde whan eteth forth auoydeth waye hath receyued thyrde whan appetyteth thynges whiche vnto hym contraryous applycacyon alyke thynge vnto dede thyrde euyll token whan desyreth thynges worldly erthly without mesure symony vsury seuenth rule phesycyan knowerit tps cum sana doctrina non sustinebut thim iiii ad tps credut et tpe teptacois tweyne tokenes helth thyrde whan mater syknes begynneth dygeste fourth whan ony maner euacuacyon man putteth humour mater whiche causen syknes applycacyon foure tokenes recouer helth spyrytuall shewed
