vnto synne thynges sayd appereth brefe applycacyon medycyne spyrytuall vnto medycyne corporall answereth one vnto well doth vnto prouffyte helth muste haue eternall amen p foloweth brefe interrogacyons man may make euery good crysten man man seeth labourynge artycle deth whiche yf may fyrste ought crysten man crysten woman byleue sted fastly ye artycles fayth vnderstonde god fader ye whiche creatour heuen erth thynges vysyble inuysyble also jhesu cryste sone whiche v hath conceyued borne vyrgyn mary whiche v teche agayne bye hath soo moche suffred payne fynally deth ryght cruell thyrde daye arose whiche styed heuen shall come agayne juge quycke deed yelde vnto euery creatour hath deserued byleue grace holy goost holy chirche sustayned nourysshed holy sacrametes ordened descesse shall aryse answere yes ye well joyfull dye crysten fayth vnyte obedyence moder holy chirche answere yes confesse ye haue poorely lyued haue deserued ony meryte goodnes yt ye better sholde haue lyued ye haue done answere yes knowlege ye ye haue offended god creatur ryght often ryght greuously answere yes haue sorowe dyspleaser synnes ye haue done godenes ye haue lefte gyftes grace god whiche ye haue well vsed answere yes haue ye good purpose wyll amende yf god graunt come vnto helth answere yes pardon good herte loue god haue offended answere yes requyre also demaude ryghte humbly pardon mercy generally yt ye haue offended answere yes byleue well yt lorde wolde dye otherwyse blessyd passyon ye may saued answere yes innumerable grace vnto hath done vnto worlde yelde ye hym grace mercy wt hert moche ye maye yf persone may speke wt fayth good conscyence herte alonely wt herte mouth togyders thynges sayd answere lyke wyse sayd suche estate desseaceth ryght grete token saluacyon persone whiche suche wyse dysposed holely hym ought recomaude comytte vnto blyssed passyon lorde puttynge therto hope meryte good dede theron ought thynke contynually moche syknes may endure bere ben surmouted beten downe dyuerse temptacyos deuyll helle man ought bytwene god fader greuousnes ye gylte synnes put oppose deth swete chyld without otherwyse pleade aledge also merytes ought haue hath ought offre merytes oure sauyoure jhesu cryste whiche ben infynyte comen vnto whiche duely axe reclayme thynke hym man sholde calle vnto mynde story ye good thefe knowleged gylte synne swetnes pyte lorde whiche requyred god fader synne whiche hym put helde tormentes deseases deth whiche co syderacyon inspyred requyre ayde jhesu cryste sayenge memento meidne saye lorde haue pyte mynde whiche thynge ought saye vnto power ye whyche laboureth extremetes deth also ought saye confyteor make protestacyon wyll dye trouth holy fayth catholyque euer illusyon freuesaye vnto hym come artycle deth afterwarde saye manus tuas dne comendo spiritum meum c p folowen vi aduysementes ryght prouffytable enduce lyuynge dye hor moche ye consystorye blyssed caplm xxix trynyte determyned irreuocably v mori et post hoc iudiciu hebre ix c daye contynually approche vnto houre ryght doubfull folowen syx aduyseme te conceyue fere whiche may dysprayse present worlde prepayre v departe surely present lyfe fyrste auysement houre deth euery creature ende worlde grete jugement vnto regarde sentence thynges whiche theder comen ben done vnto case partyculer creaturevbi te iuenio ibi te iudicabo resonable yt estate whiche man founde estate houre man jugyd sentence irreuocably vnto whiche sentence may resyste lette dyffer scyence puyssauce loue fauour ala pope emperours kynges duke erles baron euer preemynence condycyons man woman olde yonge condycyouegalle nowe acyted appere vnto suche soo meruaylous jugement full fewe whiche thynketh duely whiche thynge worldely people shewen clerely theyr lyfe holden leden whiche dampnable parte ben begyleddes morimut et quast aque delabimur terra reupttatur iii reg xiiii capitulo temptacyon deuyll whiche maketh ymagen haue true repentauce ben presented vnto jugement god vnto houre deth sayd wherforeducut bonis dy suos iputo ad ferna descedut xxi capitulo doubte contynewe theyr vayn lyfe seculer worldly whan comen vnto ende fallen justice neuer good vnto purpose make theologyens suche questyon vnderstondedecentfi milibus hoibus quo rum vita erriteri mala vix rueretur saluari vnus si vix iust saluabit impius peccator vbi pare bunt yf persone ye whiche hath ledde euyll lyfe tyll vnto syknes vnto tyme deth may come vnto good ende haue saluacyon answere saynt austen possyble whiche hath ben euyll lyfe may haue good ende ryght harde sayth eusebius one epystles hundred persones whiche haue contynued euyll lyfe cometh one vnto good ende vnto purpose sayth richarde de medium villa penaunce suffycyent vnto saluacyon whan synner hath dyspleaser synne purpose neuer consent vnto mortall synne tyme paste maketh true confessyon hole purpose place tyme vnto thynges sayd moued enduced pryncypally loue god pryncypally fere dapned occasyon seuile temporall ellys penaunce doeth artycle deth suffyseth gete saluacyon moche ryght fewe whiche haue ben euyll lyfe haue condycyons sayd houre deth foloweth whiche dyfferre taryen true penaunce tyll bedde ye tyme deth full fewe saued yf soo haue wyll loue god faythfully durynge tyme vnto gyueth moch goodes grace may body soule helth prosperyte wytte mynde goodes erthly thynges may hym loue reclayme herte pyteous tayth full whan shall holde grete dysti esle pryson greuous syknes takynge helth playes dysportes joyes gladness pleasure worldly whiche haue put theyr hertes theyr studye thynge ryght harde ymagen vnderstonde loue god true charyte whiche prouen doctours many reason fyrste grete horiyble passyon syknes fere seruyle hatefull whiche talleth espyryte humayn whiche hath god hym grace whan come suche necessyte asdfie si pauci sunt q saluaiur quam e aut dixit ad illos lote dite itrare augusta port dito vovis qr multi querat itrare potuerunt lu xiii c ite p vi e imorte memor sit tui yf ony hadde fote tyre ye water sethynge may fynde vnderstondynge reknowlege synnes grete rowe suffreth consequente may haue ye dyspleaser ye whiche necessary yt god pardoneth ye synnet gyueth grace therfore sayth well holy scrypture vnto suche people thynke god suffycyantly fynde grace whan houre deth cometh justyce reason requyren whiche hath wyll recorne vnto god promesses gyftes thretenynges increpacyons yt god hath contynued towarde thyrty fyfty yeres lesse ben predycacyos remors conscyence prosperytes worldly example andqui fecit tesine tenoiustificabit te siue te au ite greg justu vt noluit penitere cupotuit cu voluerit sero sit jugementes god ben comen theyr tyme deth whiche knowen parauenture resemb n estate maner lyuynge maners without bre vnto god called wyll retorne durynge yt hadde tyme houre ye god suffreth justly fall dampnacion eternall seeth knoweth scyence dyuine infynyte yt dayes yeres taryeth yet euer abyden obstynacyon therfore notwtstondynge yt whan ende cometh theyr necessyte wolde cofesse amende late abyde also case comenly suche penauce procedeth fere seruyle ye fere pryncypally dapned andpaucos ex credo saluari v que fine expectat iustifica ne tardescouertiad im nec diffe de die die eccle v si mutare pot et iop pelle sua et varietates suas vos poteritis v facere cu diceritis malu hi xiii therfore sayth byleueth saynt jerome suche ryght fewe saued whiche appereth clerely ynough whiche dyfferreth true parfyte penauce tyll vnto tyme deth hym dysposeth vnto dapnacyon doth agayn admonicyon holy goost seconde lettynge true penance whan ende lyfe cometh habytuacyon syne whiche soule whiche haue longely contynued euyll lyfe whiche habytuacyon ishac adue sioe cuci pctor vt mories obliuisca su du viueret oblit est dei aug vnto also naturall sholde ryght harde thynge breke dystroye put awaye whan cometh vnto ende consu macyon lyfe persone hath lytell tyme many lettynges thyrde lettynge temptacyon deuyl whiche tempteth
